    42	public final class AyaraWidowOfTheRealm extends TransformingDoubleFacedCard {
    43	
    44	    private static final DynamicValue xValue = SacrificeCostManaValue.PERMANENT;
    45	    private static final FilterPermanentOrPlayer filter = new FilterPermanentOrPlayer(
    46	            "opponent or battle", StaticFilters.FILTER_PERMANENT_BATTLE, new FilterOpponent()
    47	    );
    48	    private static final FilterCard furnaceQueenFilter = new FilterCard("artifact or creature card from your graveyard");
    49	
    50	    static {
    51	        furnaceQueenFilter.add(Predicates.or(
    52	                CardType.ARTIFACT.getPredicate(),
    53	                CardType.CREATURE.getPredicate()
    54	        ));
    55	    }

    57	    public AyaraWidowOfTheRealm(UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo) {

    59	                new SuperType[]{SuperType.LEGENDARY}, new CardType[]{CardType.CREATURE}, new SubType[]{SubType.ELF, SubType.NOBLE}, "{1}{B}{B}",
    60	                "Ayara, Furnace Queen",
    61	                new SuperType[]{SuperType.LEGENDARY}, new CardType[]{CardType.CREATURE}, new SubType[]{SubType.PHYREXIAN, SubType.ELF, SubType.NOBLE}, "BR");
    62	        this.getLeftHalfCard().setPT(3, 3);
    63	        this.getRightHalfCard().setPT(4, 4);
    64	
    65	        // {T}, Sacrifice another creature or artifact: Ayara, Widow of the Realm deals X damage to target opponent or battle and you gain X life, where X is the sacrificed permanent's mana value.
    66	        Ability ability = new SimpleActivatedAbility(new DamageTargetEffect(xValue)
    67	                .setText("{this} deals X damage to target opponent or battle"), new TapSourceCost());
    68	        ability.addCost(new SacrificeTargetCost(StaticFilters.FILTER_CONTROLLED_ANOTHER_CREATURE_OR_ARTIFACT));
    69	        ability.addEffect(new GainLifeEffect(xValue).setText("and you gain X life, where X is the sacrificed permanent's mana value"));
    70	        ability.addTarget(new TargetPermanentOrPlayer(filter));
    71	        this.getLeftHalfCard().addAbility(ability);
    72	
    73	        // {5}{R/P}: Transform Ayara. Activate only as a sorcery.
    74	        this.getLeftHalfCard().addAbility(new ActivateAsSorceryActivatedAbility(new TransformSourceEffect(), new ManaCostsImpl<>("{5}{R/P}")));
    75	
    76	        // Ayara, Furnace Queen
    77	        // At the beginning of combat on your turn, return up to one target artifact or creature card from your graveyard to the battlefield. It gains haste. Exile it at the beginning of the next end step.
    78	        Ability triggeredAbility = new BeginningOfCombatTriggeredAbility(
    79	                new AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect()
    80	        );
    81	        triggeredAbility.addTarget(new TargetCardInYourGraveyard(0, 1, furnaceQueenFilter));
    82	        this.getRightHalfCard().addAbility(triggeredAbility);
    83	    }
    84

    95	class AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    96	
    97	    AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect() {
    98	        super(Outcome.Benefit);
    99	        staticText = "return up to one target artifact or creature card from your graveyard " +
   100	                "to the battlefield. It gains haste. Exile it at the beginning of the next end step";
   101	    }

   105	    }

   109	        return new AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect(this);
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    @Override
   113	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
   114	        Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
   115	        Card card = game.getCard(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
   116	        if (player == null || card == null) {
   117	            return false;
   118	        }
   119	        Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
   120	        if (permanent == null) {
   121	            return false;
   122	        }
   123	        game.addEffect(new GainAbilityTargetEffect(
   124	                HasteAbility.getInstance(), Duration.Custom
   125	        ).setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent.getId(), game)), source);
   126	        game.addDelayedTriggeredAbility(new AtTheBeginOfNextEndStepDelayedTriggeredAbility(
   127	                new ExileTargetEffect().setText("exile it")
   128	                        .setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent.getId(), game)),
   129	                TargetController.ANY
   130	        ), source);
   131	        return true;
   132	    }

    11	import mage.cards.CardSetInfo;
    12	import mage.constants.CardType;
    13	import mage.constants.SubType;
    14	import mage.constants.Outcome;
    15	import mage.filter.StaticFilters;
    16	import mage.game.Game;
    17	import mage.game.permanent.Permanent;
    18	import mage.players.Player;
    19	import mage.target.TargetPermanent;
    20	import mage.target.common.TargetCreaturePermanent;
    21	
    22	import static mage.filter.StaticFilters.FILTER_ANOTHER_TARGET_CREATURE;
    23	
    24	/**
    25	 *
    26	 * @author fireshoes
    27	 */
    28	public final class NoxiousGearhulk extends CardImpl {
    29	
    30	    public NoxiousGearhulk(UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo) {
    31	        super(ownerId,setInfo,new CardType[]{CardType.ARTIFACT,CardType.CREATURE},"{4}{B}{B}");
    32	        this.subtype.add(SubType.CONSTRUCT);
    33	        this.power = new MageInt(5);
    34	        this.toughness = new MageInt(4);
    35	
    36	        // Menace
    37	        this.addAbility(new MenaceAbility(false));
    38	
    39	        // When Noxious Gearhulk enters the battlefield, you may destroy another target creature. If a creature is destroyed this way, you gain life equal to its toughness.
    40	        Ability ability = new EntersBattlefieldTriggeredAbility(new NoxiousGearhulkEffect());
    41	        ability.addTarget(new TargetPermanent(FILTER_ANOTHER_TARGET_CREATURE));
    42	        this.addAbility(ability);
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    private NoxiousGearhulk(final NoxiousGearhulk card) {
    46	        super(card);
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    @Override
    50	    public NoxiousGearhulk copy() {
    51	        return new NoxiousGearhulk(this);
    52	    }
    53	}
    54	
    55	class NoxiousGearhulkEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    56	
    57	    NoxiousGearhulkEffect() {
    58	        super(Outcome.DestroyPermanent);
    59	        this.staticText = "you may destroy another target creature. If a creature is destroyed this way, you gain life equal to its toughness";
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    private NoxiousGearhulkEffect(final NoxiousGearhulkEffect effect) {
    63	        super(effect);
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    @Override
    67	    public NoxiousGearhulkEffect copy() {
    68	        return new NoxiousGearhulkEffect(this);
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    @Override
    72	    public boolean apply(Game game, final Ability source) {
    73	        Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    74	        Permanent creatureToDestroy = game.getPermanent(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
    75	        if (creatureToDestroy != null && player != null) {
    76	            if (player.chooseUse(Outcome.DestroyPermanent, "Destroy creature?", source, game)) {
    77	                if (creatureToDestroy.destroy(source, game, false)) {
    78	                    player.gainLife(creatureToDestroy.getToughness().getValue(), game, source);
    79	                }
    80	            }
    81	        }
    82	        return true;
    83	    }
    84	}

    public static Permanent getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(Card card, Game game) {
        return game.getPermanent(CardUtil.getDefaultCardSideForBattlefield(game, card).getId());
    }

    /**
     * Return card name for same name searching
     *
     * @param card
     * @return
     */
    public static String getCardNameForSameNameSearch(Card card) {
        // it's ok to return one name only cause NamePredicate can find same card by first name
        if (card instanceof SplitCard) {
            return ((SplitCard) card).getLeftHalfCard().getName();
        } else if (card instanceof DoubleFacedCard) {
            return ((DoubleFacedCard) card).getLeftHalfCard().getName();
        } else {
            return card.getName();
        }
    }

    public static List<String> getCardRulesWithAdditionalInfo(MageObject object,
                                                              Abilities<Ability> rulesSource, Abilities<Ability> hintAbilities) {
        return getCardRulesWithAdditionalInfo(null, object, rulesSource, hintAbilities);
    }

    public static Card getDefaultCardSideForBattlefield(Game game, Card card) {
        if (card instanceof PermanentCard) {
            return card;
        }

        // must choose left side all time
        Card permCard;
        if (card instanceof SplitCard) {
            permCard = card;
        } else if (card instanceof CardWithSpellOption) {
            permCard = card;
        } else if (card instanceof DoubleFacedCard) {
            permCard = ((DoubleFacedCard) card).getLeftHalfCard();
        } else {
            permCard = card;
        }

        // original code checked to ensure card not instant or sorcery
        // but that's not correct, e.g. manifest with Fierce Invocation
        // must not throw error in that case, just continue

        return permCard;
    }

    /**
     * If a card object is moved to the battlefield, object id can be different (e.g. MDFC).
     * Use this method to get the permanent object from the card object after move to battlefield.
     * Can return null if not found on the battlefield.
     */
    public static Permanent getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(Card card, Game game) {
        return game.getPermanent(CardUtil.getDefaultCardSideForBattlefield(game, card).getId());

    13	
    14	    public TransformingDoubleFacedCard(
    15	            UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo,
    16	            CardType[] typesLeft, SubType[] subTypesLeft, String costsLeft,
    17	            String secondSideName,
    18	            CardType[] typesRight, SubType[] subTypesRight, String colorRight

    21	                ownerId, setInfo,

    25	        );
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    public TransformingDoubleFacedCard(
    29	            UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo,
    30	            SuperType[] superTypesLeft, CardType[] typesLeft, SubType[] subTypesLeft, String costsLeft,
    31	            String secondSideName,
    32	            SuperType[] superTypesRight, CardType[] typesRight, SubType[] subTypesRight, String colorRight
    33	    ) {
    34	        super(ownerId, setInfo, typesLeft, costsLeft, SpellAbilityType.TRANSFORMED);
    35	        // main card name must be same as left side
    36	        leftHalfCard = new TransformingDoubleFacedCardHalf(
    37	                this.getOwnerId(), setInfo.copy(),
    38	                superTypesLeft, typesLeft, subTypesLeft, costsLeft,
    39	                this, SpellAbilityType.TRANSFORMED_LEFT
    40	        );
    41	        rightHalfCard = new TransformingDoubleFacedCardHalf(
    42	                this.getOwnerId(), new CardSetInfo(secondSideName, setInfo),
    43	                superTypesRight, typesRight, subTypesRight, colorRight, this
    44	        );
    45	        this.secondSideCard = rightHalfCard;
    46	    }

    49	        super(card);
    50	    }

    54	        if (ability.getSpellAbilityType() == SpellAbilityType.BASE) {
    55	            return this.leftHalfCard.cast(game, fromZone, ability, controllerId);
    56	        }
    57	        return super.cast(game, fromZone, ability, controllerId);
    58	    }

    21	/**
    22	 * @author JayDi85 - originally from ModalDoubleFaceCard
    23	 */
    24	public abstract class DoubleFacedCard extends CardImpl implements CardWithHalves {
    25	
    26	    protected DoubleFacedCardHalf leftHalfCard; // main card in all zone
    27	    protected DoubleFacedCardHalf rightHalfCard; // second side card, can be only in stack and battlefield zones
    28	
    29	    protected DoubleFacedCard(UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo, CardType[] cardTypes, String costs, SpellAbilityType spellAbilityType) {
    30	        super(ownerId, setInfo, cardTypes, costs, spellAbilityType);
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    public DoubleFacedCard(DoubleFacedCard card) {
    34	        super(card);
    35	        // make sure all parts created and parent ref added
    36	        this.leftHalfCard = (DoubleFacedCardHalf) card.getLeftHalfCard().copy();
    37	        leftHalfCard.setParentCard(this);
    38	        this.rightHalfCard = (DoubleFacedCardHalf) card.getRightHalfCard().copy();
    39	        rightHalfCard.setParentCard(this);
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    public abstract DoubleFacedCardHalf getLeftHalfCard();
    43	
    44	    public abstract DoubleFacedCardHalf getRightHalfCard();
    45	
    46	    public void setParts(DoubleFacedCardHalf leftHalfCard, DoubleFacedCardHalf rightHalfCard) {
    47	        // for card copy only - set new parts
    48	        this.leftHalfCard = leftHalfCard;
    49	        leftHalfCard.setParentCard(this);
    50	        this.rightHalfCard = rightHalfCard;
    51	        rightHalfCard.setParentCard(this);
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    @Override
    55	    public void assignNewId() {

    66	    }
    67	
    68	    private void setSideZones(Zone mainZone, Game game) {
    69	        switch (mainZone) {
    70	            case BATTLEFIELD:
    71	            case STACK:
    72	                throw new IllegalArgumentException("Wrong code usage: you must put to battlefield/stack only real side card (half), not main");
    73	            default:
    74	                game.setZone(leftHalfCard.getId(), mainZone);
    75	                game.setZone(rightHalfCard.getId(), mainZone);
    76	                break;
    77	        }
    78	        checkGoodZones(game, this);
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    @Override
    82	    public boolean moveToZone(Zone toZone, Ability source, Game game, boolean flag, List<UUID> appliedEffects) {
    83	        if (super.moveToZone(toZone, source, game, flag, appliedEffects)) {
    84	            Zone currentZone = game.getState().getZone(getId());
    85	            setSideZones(currentZone, game);
    86	            return true;
    87	        }
    88	        return false;
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    @Override
    92	    public void setZone(Zone zone, Game game) {
    93	        super.setZone(zone, game);
    94	        setSideZones(zone, game);
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    @Override
    98	    public boolean moveToExile(UUID exileId, String name, Ability source, Game game, List<UUID> appliedEffects) {
    99	        if (super.moveToExile(exileId, name, source, game, appliedEffects)) {
   100	            Zone currentZone = game.getState().getZone(getId());
   101	            setSideZones(currentZone, game);
   102	            return true;
   103	        }
   104	        return false;
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    /**
   108	     * Runtime check for good zones and other MDF data
   109	     */
   110	    public static void checkGoodZones(Game game, DoubleFacedCard card) {
   111	        Card leftPart = card.getLeftHalfCard();
   112	        Card rightPart = card.getRightHalfCard();
   113	
   114	        Zone zoneMain = game.getState().getZone(card.getId());
   115	        Zone zoneLeft = game.getState().getZone(leftPart.getId());
   116	        Zone zoneRight = game.getState().getZone(rightPart.getId());
   117	
   118	        // runtime check:
   119	        // * in battlefield and stack - card + one of the sides (another side in outside zone)
   120	        // * in other zones - card + both sides (need both sides due cost reductions, spell and other access before put to stack)
   121	        //
   122	        // 712.8a While a double-faced card is outside the game or in a zone other than the battlefield or stack,
   123	        // it has only the characteristics of its front face.
   124	        //
   125	        // 712.8f While a modal double-faced spell is on the stack or a modal double-faced permanent is on the battlefield,
   126	        // it has only the characteristics of the face that’s up.
   127	        Zone needZoneLeft;
   128	        Zone needZoneRight;
   129	        switch (zoneMain) {
   130	            case BATTLEFIELD:
   131	            case STACK:
   132	                if (zoneMain == zoneLeft) {
   133	                    needZoneLeft = zoneMain;
   134	                    needZoneRight = Zone.OUTSIDE;
   135	                } else if (zoneMain == zoneRight) {
   136	                    needZoneLeft = Zone.OUTSIDE;
   137	                    needZoneRight = zoneMain;
   138	                } else {
   139	                    // impossible
   140	                    needZoneLeft = zoneMain;
   141	                    needZoneRight = Zone.OUTSIDE;
   142	                }
   143	                break;
   144	            default:
   145	                needZoneLeft = zoneMain;
   146	                needZoneRight = zoneMain;
   147	                break;
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        if (zoneLeft != needZoneLeft || zoneRight != needZoneRight) {
   151	            throw new IllegalStateException("Wrong code usage: MDF card uses wrong zones - " + card
   152	                    + "\r\n" + String.format("* main zone: %s", zoneMain)
   153	                    + "\r\n" + String.format("* left side: need %s, actual %s", needZoneLeft, zoneLeft)
   154	                    + "\r\n" + String.format("* right side: need %s, actual %s", needZoneRight, zoneRight));
   155	        }
   156	    }
   157

   260	
   261	    private boolean isIgnoreDefaultAbility(Ability ability) {
   262	        // ignore default play/spell ability from main card (only halves are actual)
   263	        // default abilities added on card creation from card type and can't be skipped
   264	
   265	        // skip cast spell
   266	        if (ability instanceof SpellAbility) {
   267	            SpellAbilityType type = ((SpellAbility) ability).getSpellAbilityType();
   268	            return type == SpellAbilityType.MODAL || type == SpellAbilityType.TRANSFORMED;
   269	        }
   270	
   271	        // skip play land
   272	        return ability instanceof PlayLandAbility;
   273	    }
   274	
   275	    private boolean isIgnoreTransformSpellAbility(Ability ability) {
   276	        return ability instanceof SpellAbility && ((SpellAbility) ability).getSpellAbilityType() == SpellAbilityType.TRANSFORMED_RIGHT;
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    private Abilities<Ability> getInnerAbilities(Game game, boolean showLeftSide, boolean showRightSide) {
   280	        Abilities<Ability> allAbilites = new AbilitiesImpl<>();
   281	
   282	        for (Ability ability : super.getAbilities(game)) {
   283	            if (isIgnoreDefaultAbility(ability)) {
   284	                continue;
   285	            }
   286	            allAbilites.add(ability);
   287	        }
   288	
   289	        if (showLeftSide) {
   290	            allAbilites.addAll(leftHalfCard.getAbilities(game));
   291	        }
   292	        if (showRightSide) {
   293	            for (Ability ability: rightHalfCard.getAbilities(game)) {
   294	                if (isIgnoreTransformSpellAbility(ability)) {
   295	                    continue;
   296	                }
   297	                allAbilites.add(ability);
   298	            }
   299	        }
   300	
   301	        return allAbilites;
   302	    }
   303	
   304	    private Abilities<Ability> getInnerAbilities(boolean showLeftSide, boolean showRightSide) {
   305	        Abilities<Ability> allAbilites = new AbilitiesImpl<>();
   306	
   307	        for (Ability ability : super.getAbilities()) {
   308	            if (isIgnoreDefaultAbility(ability)) {
   309	                continue;
   310	            }
   311	            allAbilites.add(ability);
   312	        }
   313	
   314	        if (showLeftSide) {
   315	            allAbilites.addAll(leftHalfCard.getAbilities());
   316	        }
   317	
   318	        if (showRightSide) {
   319	            for (Ability ability: rightHalfCard.getAbilities()) {
   320	                if (isIgnoreTransformSpellAbility(ability)) {
   321	                    continue;
   322	                }
   323	                allAbilites.add(ability);
   324	            }
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        return allAbilites;
   328	    }

   330	    @Override
   331	    public List<String> getRules() {
   332	        // rules must show only main side (another side visible by toggle/transform button in GUI)
   333	        // card hints from both sides
   334	        return CardUtil.getCardRulesWithAdditionalInfo(
   335	                this,
   336	                this.getInnerAbilities(true, false),
   337	                this.getInnerAbilities(true, true)
   338	        );
   339	    }

   344	        // card hints from both sides

   346	                game,

   349	                this.getInnerAbilities(game, true, true)

     3	import mage.abilities.Ability;

     8	import mage.cards.Card;
     9	import mage.constants.Duration;
    10	import mage.constants.Outcome;
    11	import mage.constants.TargetController;
    12	import mage.constants.Zone;
    13	import mage.filter.FilterCard;
    14	import mage.game.Game;
    15	import mage.game.permanent.Permanent;
    16	import mage.players.Player;
    17	import mage.target.common.TargetCardInHand;
    18	import mage.target.targetpointer.FixedTarget;
    19	import mage.util.CardUtil;
    20	
    21	/**
    22	 * @author TheElk801
    23	 */
    24	public class PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    25	
    26	    private final FilterCard filter;
    27	    private final Duration duration;
    28	
    29	    public PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect(FilterCard filter, Duration duration, String objectName, String objectName2) {
    30	        super(Outcome.PutCreatureInPlay);
    31	        this.filter = filter;
    32	        this.duration = duration;
    33	        this.staticText = "you may put " + CardUtil.addArticle(filter.getMessage()) +
    34	                " from your hand onto the battlefield. " + objectName +
    35	                " gains haste" + (duration.toString().isEmpty() ? "" : ' ' + duration.toString()) +
    36	                ". Sacrifice " + objectName2 + " at the beginning of the next end step";
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    private PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect(final PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect effect) {
    40	        super(effect);
    41	        this.filter = effect.filter;
    42	        this.duration = effect.duration;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    @Override
    46	    public PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect copy() {
    47	        return new PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect(this);
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    @Override
    51	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    52	        Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    53	        if (player == null) {
    54	            return false;
    55	        }
    56	        TargetCardInHand target = new TargetCardInHand(0, 1, filter);
    57	        player.choose(outcome, target, source, game);
    58	        Card card = game.getCard(target.getFirstTarget());
    59	        if (card == null) {
    60	            return false;
    61	        }
    62	        player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game);
    63	        Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
    64	        if (permanent == null) {
    65	            return false;
    66	        }
    67	        game.addEffect(new GainAbilityTargetEffect(HasteAbility.getInstance(), duration)
    68	                .setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent, game)), source);
    69	        game.addDelayedTriggeredAbility(new AtTheBeginOfNextEndStepDelayedTriggeredAbility(
    70	                new SacrificeTargetEffect("sacrifice it")
    71	                        .setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent, game)),
    72	                TargetController.ANY
    73	        ), source);
    74	        return true;
    75	    }
    76	}

    23	    }

    public boolean moveCards(Card card, Zone toZone, Ability source, Game game) {
        return moveCards(card, toZone, source, game, false, false, false, null);

    @Override
    public boolean moveCards(Card card, Zone toZone, Ability source, Game game, boolean tapped, boolean faceDown, boolean byOwner, List<UUID> appliedEffects) {
        Set<Card> cardList = new HashSet<>();
        if (card != null) {
            cardList.add(card);
        }
        return moveCards(cardList, toZone, source, game, tapped, faceDown, byOwner, appliedEffects);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean moveCards(Cards cards, Zone toZone, Ability source, Game game) {
        return moveCards(cards.getCards(game), toZone, source, game);
    }

    @Override
    public boolean moveCards(Set<? extends Card> cards, Zone toZone,
                             Ability source, Game game
    ) {
        return moveCards(cards, toZone, source, game, false, false, false, null);
    }

I notice something important. In `AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect.apply()`:

```java
Card card = game.getCard(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
```

The target pointer gets the first target from the game/source. But the effect also needs to move the card. Let me look at how `moveCards` is called - actually, it seems like in this effect, there is NO call to `moveCards`! 

Wait, let me re-read the effect:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    Card card = game.getCard(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
    if (player == null || card == null) {
        return false;
    }
    Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
    if (permanent == null) {
        return false;
    }
    ...
}
```

There's no `moveCards` call! The card is never moved from graveyard to battlefield. Let me compare with `ReturnCreatureFromGraveyardToBattlefieldAndGainHasteEffect`:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    if (controller == null) {
        return false;
    }
    Card card = game.getCard(source.getFirstTarget());
    if (card != null) {
        controller.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game);  // <-- THIS moves the card
        Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
        ...
    }
    return false;
}
```

Yes! The `AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect` is missing the call to `controller.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)`! It just gets the card from the graveyard and tries to get a permanent from it without actually moving it to the battlefield first.

Let me also check `PutCardIntoPlayWithHasteAndSacrificeEffect`:
```java
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game);
Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
```

Both similar effects call `moveCards` before `getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield`. The AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect is missing this crucial step!

Let me verify this by looking at the full effect again and comparing with other similar cards

    30	    private static final FilterCard filter = new FilterCard("creature or Vehicle card from your graveyard");
    31	
    32	    static {
    33	        filter.add(Predicates.or(
    34	                CardType.CREATURE.getPredicate(),
    35	                SubType.VEHICLE.getPredicate()
    36	        ));
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    public OkibaSalvage(UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo) {
    40	        super(ownerId, setInfo, new CardType[]{CardType.SORCERY}, "{4}{B}");
    41	
    42	        // Return target creature or Vehicle card from your graveyard to the battlefield. Then put two +1/+1 counters on that permanent if you control an artifact and an enchantment.
    43	        this.getSpellAbility().addEffect(new OkibaSalvageEffect());
    44	        this.getSpellAbility().addTarget(new TargetCardInYourGraveyard(filter));
    45	        this.getSpellAbility().addHint(ControlArtifactAndEnchantmentHint.instance);
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    private OkibaSalvage(final OkibaSalvage card) {
    49	        super(card);
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    @Override
    53	    public OkibaSalvage copy() {
    54	        return new OkibaSalvage(this);
    55	    }
    56	}
    57	
    58	class OkibaSalvageEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    59	
    60	    OkibaSalvageEffect() {
    61	        super(Outcome.Benefit);
    62	        staticText = "return target creature or Vehicle card from your graveyard to the battlefield. " +
    63	                "Then put two +1/+1 counters on that permanent if you control an artifact and an enchantment";
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    private OkibaSalvageEffect(final OkibaSalvageEffect effect) {
    67	        super(effect);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    @Override
    71	    public OkibaSalvageEffect copy() {
    72	        return new OkibaSalvageEffect(this);
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    @Override
    76	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    77	        Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    78	        Card card = game.getCard(source.getFirstTarget());
    79	        if (player == null || card == null) {
    80	            return false;
    81	        }
    82	        player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game);
    83	        Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
    84	        if (permanent != null && ControlArtifactAndEnchantmentCondition.instance.apply(game, source)) {
    85	            permanent.addCounters(CounterType.P1P1.createInstance(2), source, game);
    86	        }
    87	        return true;
    88	    }
    89	}

    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * @author TheElk801
    41	 */
    42	public final class AyaraWidowOfTheRealm extends TransformingDoubleFacedCard {
    43	
    44	    private static final DynamicValue xValue = SacrificeCostManaValue.PERMANENT;
    45	    private static final FilterPermanentOrPlayer filter = new FilterPermanentOrPlayer(
    46	            "opponent or battle", StaticFilters.FILTER_PERMANENT_BATTLE, new FilterOpponent()
    47	    );
    48	    private static final FilterCard furnaceQueenFilter = new FilterCard("artifact or creature card from your graveyard");
    49	
    50	    static {
    51	        furnaceQueenFilter.add(Predicates.or(
    52	                CardType.ARTIFACT.getPredicate(),
    53	                CardType.CREATURE.getPredicate()
    54	        ));
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    public AyaraWidowOfTheRealm(UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo) {
    58	        super(ownerId, setInfo,
    59	                new SuperType[]{SuperType.LEGENDARY}, new CardType[]{CardType.CREATURE}, new SubType[]{SubType.ELF, SubType.NOBLE}, "{1}{B}{B}",
    60	                "Ayara, Furnace Queen",
    61	                new SuperType[]{SuperType.LEGENDARY}, new CardType[]{CardType.CREATURE}, new SubType[]{SubType.PHYREXIAN, SubType.ELF, SubType.NOBLE}, "BR");
    62	        this.getLeftHalfCard().setPT(3, 3);
    63	        this.getRightHalfCard().setPT(4, 4);
    64	
    65	        // {T}, Sacrifice another creature or artifact: Ayara, Widow of the Realm deals X damage to target opponent or battle and you gain X life, where X is the sacrificed permanent's mana value.
    66	        Ability ability = new SimpleActivatedAbility(new DamageTargetEffect(xValue)
    67	                .setText("{this} deals X damage to target opponent or battle"), new TapSourceCost());
    68	        ability.addCost(new SacrificeTargetCost(StaticFilters.FILTER_CONTROLLED_ANOTHER_CREATURE_OR_ARTIFACT));
    69	        ability.addEffect(new GainLifeEffect(xValue).setText("and you gain X life, where X is the sacrificed permanent's mana value"));
    70	        ability.addTarget(new TargetPermanentOrPlayer(filter));
    71	        this.getLeftHalfCard().addAbility(ability);
    72	
    73	        // {5}{R/P}: Transform Ayara. Activate only as a sorcery.
    74	        this.getLeftHalfCard().addAbility(new ActivateAsSorceryActivatedAbility(new TransformSourceEffect(), new ManaCostsImpl<>("{5}{R/P}")));
    75	
    76	        // Ayara, Furnace Queen
    77	        // At the beginning of combat on your turn, return up to one target artifact or creature card from your graveyard to the battlefield. It gains haste. Exile it at the beginning of the next end step.
    78	        Ability triggeredAbility = new BeginningOfCombatTriggeredAbility(
    79	                new AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect()
    80	        );
    81	        triggeredAbility.addTarget(new TargetCardInYourGraveyard(0, 1, furnaceQueenFilter));
    82	        this.getRightHalfCard().addAbility(triggeredAbility);
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    private AyaraWidowOfTheRealm(final AyaraWidowOfTheRealm card) {
    86	        super(card);
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    @Override
    90	    public AyaraWidowOfTheRealm copy() {
    91	        return new AyaraWidowOfTheRealm(this);
    92	    }
    93	}
    94	
    95	class AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    96	
    97	    AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect() {
    98	        super(Outcome.Benefit);
    99	        staticText = "return up to one target artifact or creature card from your graveyard " +
   100	                "to the battlefield. It gains haste. Exile it at the beginning of the next end step";
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    private AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect(final AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect effect) {
   104	        super(effect);
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    @Override
   108	    public AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect copy() {
   109	        return new AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect(this);
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    @Override
   113	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
   114	        Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
   115	        Card card = game.getCard(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
   116	        if (player == null || card == null) {
   117	            return false;
   118	        }
   119	        Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
   120	        if (permanent == null) {
   121	            return false;
   122	        }
   123	        game.addEffect(new GainAbilityTargetEffect(
   124	                HasteAbility.getInstance(), Duration.Custom
   125	        ).setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent.getId(), game)), source);
   126	        game.addDelayedTriggeredAbility(new AtTheBeginOfNextEndStepDelayedTriggeredAbility(
   127	                new ExileTargetEffect().setText("exile it")
   128	                        .setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent.getId(), game)),
   129	                TargetController.ANY
   130	        ), source);
   131	        return true;
   132	    }
   133	}

Good, the build passes. Now let me think about edge cases.

Looking at the fix, the issue was that the `AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect.apply()` method was missing the call to `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)` to actually move the card from the graveyard to the battlefield. Without this call, `CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game)` would return null because the card is still in the graveyard, not on the battlefield.

Let me also look at the `ReturnCreatureFromGraveyardToBattlefieldAndGainHasteEffect` to verify the pattern is the same:

```java
// ReturnCreatureFromGraveyardToBattlefieldAndGainHasteEffect (correct pattern):
Card card = game.getCard(source.getFirstTarget());
if (card != null) {
    controller.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game);
    Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
    ...
}
```

Our fix now matches this pattern:

```java
// AyaraFurnaceQueenEffect (after fix):
Card card = game.getCard(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
if (player == null || card == null) {
    return false;
}
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game);  // ADDED
Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
...
```

Now let me also check if there's a potential issue with the fact that this is an "up to one" target (0 or 1). The `TargetCardInYourGraveyard(0, 1, ...)` allows choosing 0 targets. If no target is chosen, `getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source)` should return null, and the card would be null, so it would return false early (which is correct - nothing to return).

Let me also verify the behavior when the card is a DFC (like Ayara itself). The `moveCards` method should handle DFCs correctly as it's a standard method used by many other cards.

One more thing to check - let me look at the `ReturnCreatureFromGraveyardToBattlefieldAndGainHasteEffect` and see how it differs from our effect. Our effect also adds the exile at beginning of next end step, which is additional functionality.

Let me also look at other similar effects in the codebase that return from graveyard with haste + exile at end step to see if there's any other nuance

    30	/**
    31	 *
    32	 * @author spjspj

    34	public final class ApprenticeNecromancer extends CardImpl {
    35	
    36	    public ApprenticeNecromancer(UUID ownerId, CardSetInfo setInfo) {
    37	        super(ownerId, setInfo, new CardType[]{CardType.CREATURE}, "{1}{B}");
    38	
    39	        this.subtype.add(SubType.ZOMBIE);
    40	        this.subtype.add(SubType.WIZARD);
    41	        this.power = new MageInt(1);
    42	        this.toughness = new MageInt(1);
    43	
    44	        // {B}, {tap}, Sacrifice Apprentice Necromancer: Return target creature card from your graveyard to the battlefield. That creature gains haste. At the beginning of the next end step, sacrifice it.
    45	        Ability ability = new SimpleActivatedAbility(new ApprenticeNecromancerEffect(), new ColoredManaCost(ColoredManaSymbol.B));
    46	        ability.addCost(new TapSourceCost());
    47	        ability.addCost(new SacrificeSourceCost());
    48	        ability.addTarget(new TargetCardInYourGraveyard(StaticFilters.FILTER_CARD_CREATURE_YOUR_GRAVEYARD));
    49	        this.addAbility(ability);
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    private ApprenticeNecromancer(final ApprenticeNecromancer card) {
    53	        super(card);
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    @Override
    57	    public ApprenticeNecromancer copy() {
    58	        return new ApprenticeNecromancer(this);
    59	    }
    60	}
    61	
    62	class ApprenticeNecromancerEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    63	
    64	    ApprenticeNecromancerEffect() {
    65	        super(Outcome.PutCreatureInPlay);
    66	        this.staticText = "Return target creature card from your graveyard to the battlefield. That creature gains haste. At the beginning of the next end step, sacrifice it";
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    private ApprenticeNecromancerEffect(final ApprenticeNecromancerEffect effect) {
    70	        super(effect);
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    @Override
    74	    public ApprenticeNecromancerEffect copy() {
    75	        return new ApprenticeNecromancerEffect(this);
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    @Override
    79	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    80	        Card card = game.getCard(this.getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
    81	        Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    82	        if (controller != null && card != null) {
    83	            if (controller.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)) {
    84	                Permanent creature = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
    85	                if (creature != null) {
    86	                    // Gains haste
    87	                    ContinuousEffect effect = new GainAbilityTargetEffect(HasteAbility.getInstance(), Duration.Custom);
    88	                    effect.setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(creature, game));
    89	                    game.addEffect(effect, source);
    90	
    91	                    // Sacrifice at beginning of next end step
    92	                    SacrificeTargetEffect sacrificeEffect = new SacrificeTargetEffect("sacrifice the creature", source.getControllerId());
    93	                    sacrificeEffect.setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(creature, game));
    94	                    DelayedTriggeredAbility delayedAbility = new AtTheBeginOfNextEndStepDelayedTriggeredAbility(sacrificeEffect);
    95	                    game.addDelayedTriggeredAbility(delayedAbility, source);
    96	                }
    97	            }
    98	            return true;
    99	        }
   100	        return false;
   101	    }
   102	}

I see that `ApprenticeNecromancer` has the same pattern - it calls `controller.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)` before getting the permanent. And it also checks the return value of `moveCards`.

Now there's a subtle difference: `ApprenticeNecromancer` checks `if (controller.moveCards(...))` and nests the permanent retrieval inside. Our fix doesn't check the return value of `moveCards`. But looking at other examples like `OkibaSalvageEffect`, they also don't check the return value. The `moveCards` method returns false if cards are empty, but we already check `card == null` before. And `getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield` will return null if the move didn't succeed, which is handled by the null check.

So our fix is consistent with `OkibaSalvageEffect` pattern, which is also by `@author TheElk801` (same as Ayara).

2026-05-30 06:36:01,474 - INFO - swea-agent-magefree__mage-14655 - 💭 THOUGHT
The build succeeds. Let me now submit.

Actually, let me think about this more carefully. The PR description says:

> "transformed Ayara during main phase 1. Targeted Noxious Gearhulk (who had died during that first main phase to her sacrifice other side). Noxious Gearhulk failed to return to the battlefield."

So the scenario is:
1. Player has Ayara, Widow of the Realm on the battlefield
2. Player also has Noxious Gearhulk on the battlefield
3. Player activates Ayara's first ability: {T}, Sacrifice another creature or artifact: Ayara deals X damage... 
4. Player sacrifices Noxious Gearhulk as part of the cost (it dies and goes to graveyard)
5. Later in the same main phase, player activates Ayara's transform ability: {5}{R/P}: Transform Ayara
6. Ayara transforms to Ayara, Furnace Queen
7. Combat phase begins, triggering Ayara, Furnace Queen's ability
8. Player targets Noxious Gearhulk in graveyard
9. Noxious Gearhulk fails to return

Our fix adds the missing `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)` call which moves the card from graveyard to battlefield. Without it, the effect would look for the card on the battlefield (via `getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield`) while it's still in the graveyard, resulting in null and the effect returning false.

This fix is correct and minimal.
